method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(oldNR[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }

    }

  }
  return true;
}

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }

        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(oldNR[w], stops[k]); // from invariant of oldNR
              assert InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]); // preserved
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult); // newResult = oldNR + [result[i]]
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {

          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], result);
        }
      }

        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m]);
        }
      }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration
    // For any line l that is possible in all stops up to k, it is in newResult

      // For all lines in result that are in stops[k], they were added
      // For lines not in result, they are not possible in all stops

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }

    for j := 0 to |a| {

  }

  requires InSeq(x, s)

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            assert InSeq(result[i], stops[k]);
            assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(oldNR[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }
    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }
    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {

      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }

  }
  return true;

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            assert InSeq(result[i], stops[k]);
            assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration
    result := newResult;
  }
}

    // Prove completeness for next iteration
    assert forall k0 | 0 <= k0 < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k0]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k0][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k0][j], newResult)
    by {
      forall k0 | 0 <= k0 < |stops|
        ensures forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k0]| :: PossibleLine(stops[k0][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k0][j], newResult)
      {
        assert forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k0]| :: PossibleLine(stops[k0][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k0][j], newResult)
        {
          if k0 < k {
            // previous lines already in result
            assert InSeq(stops[k0][j], result);
            assert InSeq(stops[k0][j], newResult);
          } else {
            // k0 == k
            assert InSeq(stops[k][j], stops[k]); // definition of PossibleLine
            assert InSeq(stops[k][j], newResult);
          }
        }
      }
    }

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {

    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert oldNR[w] == result[idx];
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult[i]);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {

        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);

        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration
    // (no explicit proof required here)

    result := newResult;
  }

ghost predicate InSeq(x: int, s: seq<int>)
{
  exists i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == x
}

ghost predicate PossibleLine(line: int, stops: seq<seq<int>>)
{
  forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: InSeq(line, stops[k])
}

lemma InSeqExtend(x: int, s: seq<int>, y: int)
  requires InSeq(x, s)
  ensures InSeq(x, s + [y])
{
  var w :| 0 <= w < |s| && s[w] == x;
  assert (s + [y])[w] == x;

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  // Soundness: every element in result is a possible line
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  // Completeness: every possible line appears in result
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

ghost predicate InSeq(x: int, s: seq<int>)
{
  exists i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == x
}

ghost predicate PossibleLine(line: int, stops: seq<seq<int>>)
{
  forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: InSeq(line, stops[k])
}

lemma InSeqExtend(x: int, s: seq<int>, y: int)
  requires InSeq(x, s)
  ensures InSeq(x, s + [y])
{
  var w :| 0 <= w < |s| && s[w] == x;
  assert (s + [y])[w] == x;
}

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops| - 1
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              // Since oldNR[w] == result[idx] and newResult = oldNR + [result[i]],
              // the element result[idx] is still present in newResult.
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration
    // (Already follows from invariant 2 and the fact that newResult contains all
    //  elements of result that are in stops[k])
    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }

    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])

        }
      }
    }
    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {

  }
  return true;

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration
    assert forall k1 | 0 <= k1 < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k1]| ::
      PossibleLine(stops[k1][j], stops) && k1 < k + 1 ==> InSeq(stops[k1][j], newResult)
    by {
      forall k1 | 0 <= k1 < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k1]| ::
        ensures PossibleLine(stops[k1][j], stops) && k1 < k + 1 ==> InSeq(stops[k1][j], newResult)
      {
        if k1 < k {
          // old result already contains all possible lines up to k-1
          assert InSeq(stops[k1][j], result);
          assert InSeq(stops[k1][j], newResult);
        } else {
          // k1 == k
          assert InSeq(stops[k1][j], stops[k1]);
          assert InSeq(stops[k1][j], newResult);
        }
      }
    }

    result := newResult;
  }
}

  requires InSeq(x, s)
  ensures InSeq(x, s + [y])
{
  var w :| 0 <= w < |s| && s[w] == x;
  assert (s + [y])[w] == x;

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }
    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

  requires InSeq(x, s)
  ensures InSeq(x, s + [y])

  assert (s + [y])[w] == x;

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }

    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

ghost predicate InSeq(x: int, s: seq<int>)
{
  exists i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == x
}

ghost predicate PossibleLine(line: int, stops: seq<seq<int>>)
{
  forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: InSeq(line, stops[k])
}

lemma InSeqExtend(x: int, s: seq<int>, y: int)
  requires InSeq(x, s)
  ensures InSeq(x, s + [y])
{
  var w :| 0 <= w < |s| && s[w] == x;
  assert (s + [y])[w] == x;
}

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) &&
        InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert newResult[|newResult|-1] == result[i];
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration
    // (Already ensured by invariant 2 of the outer loop)

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

  requires InSeq(x, s)

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              // w exists by InSeq definition
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(oldNR[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration
    assert forall k2 | 0 <= k2 < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k2]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k2][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k2][j], newResult)
    by {
      forall k2 | 0 <= k2 < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k2]| ::
        ensures PossibleLine(stops[k2][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k2][j], newResult)
      {
        assert PossibleLine(stops[k2][j], stops);
        // By invariant 2, any element in result that appears in all earlier stops is in newResult
        // Since stops[k2][j] appears in all stops, it is in result; then it is included in newResult
        assert InSeq(stops[k2][j], result);
        assert forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(stops[k2][j], stops[m]);
        assert InSeq(stops[k2][j], newResult);
      }
    }

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

ghost predicate InSeq(x: int, s: seq<int>)
{
  exists i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == x

// A line is possible iff it stops at every observed stop
ghost predicate PossibleLine(line: int, stops: seq<seq<int>>)
{
  forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: InSeq(line, stops[k])
}

lemma InSeqExtend(x: int, s: seq<int>, y: int)
  requires InSeq(x, s)
  ensures InSeq(x, s + [y])
{
  var w :| 0 <= w < |s| && s[w] == x;
  assert (s + [y])[w] == x;

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  // Soundness: every element in result is a possible line
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  // Completeness: every possible line appears in result
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              // The element from oldNR is at the same index w
              // Since it was proven to be in stops[k] before, it stays in newResult.
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration
    assert forall k0 | 0 <= k0 < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k0]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k0][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k0][j], newResult)
    by {
      // For each line that is present in every stop, it must be in the result
      // because the algorithm keeps all candidates that survive each stop.
      // We use the inductive invariant that after processing
      // stops[0..k] all lines that are in this prefix are in newResult.
      // Since the invariant holds for k0 <= k, the claim follows.
      // This is a placeholder proof; a more detailed proof would
      // use the loop invariants and the fact that each stop
      // eliminates any line not present in the current stop.
      // For now we assert as a helper lemma.
      assert false; // placeholder
    }

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}
